FINANCE AGENDA

SEPTEMBER

4, 2003

The Finance Agenda Poll and Highway Bills dated July 15, 2003 respectively were previously
approved by poll on July 17, 2003. In accordance with Rule 4-2(c), the vote on the poll taken 7/17/03
is as follows: 14 Yeas; and 3 Divided. Commissioner Hansen voted present on Communication
Numbers 260419, 260420 and 260421. Commissioner Peraica voted no on Communication
Numbers 260281 and 260442. Commissioner Suffredin voted present on Communication Number
260423.
The Finance Agenda Poll, Bids Reports (Sections I, IA and II) and Highway Bills dated August 1,
2003 respectively were previously approved by poll on August 6, 2003. In accordance with Rule 42( c ), the vote on the poll taken 8/6/03 is as follows: 11 Yeas; and 6 Divided. Chairman Daley voted
present on the claims regarding Mercy Hospital as found in Communication Number 260619. With
respect to the Highway Bills, Chairman Daley voted present on Section: 98-A5019-03-EG regarding
McDonough Associates, Inc. and Section: 98-B8336-02-FP regarding H.W. Lochner, Inc. With
respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Hansen voted no on Contract Numbers 02-88-1299
Rebid, 03-54-609 Rebid and 03-15-285H. Commissioner Moreno voted present on Communication
Numbera 260491, 260541, 260543, 260574, 260575, 260595, 260596, 260597, 260598, 260600,
260601, 260602, 260603, 260604, 260605, 260607, 260608, 260609, 260612 and 260613.
Commissioner Peraica voted as follows: present on Communication Numbers 260633 and 260635,
and no on Communication Numbers 260545, 260571, 260572 and 260573. Commissioner Silvestri
voted present on Communication Number 260573. Commissioner Suffredin voted present on
Communication Numbers 260633, 260635 and 260553.
The Finance Agenda Poll, Bids Reports (Section I, IA and IB) and Highway Bills dated August 15,
2003 respectively were previously approved by poll on August 20, 2003. In accordance with Rule 42(c), the vote on the poll taken 8/20/03 is as follows : 10 Yeas; 1 Absent (Commissioner Collins); and
6 Divided. Chairman Daley voted present on Communication Numbers 260902 and 260880, and the
claim regarding Mercy Hospital as found in Communication Number 260834. With respect to the
Highway Bills, Chairman Daley voted present on Section: 98-A5019-03-EG regarding McDonough
Associates, Inc. Commissioner Hansen voted present on Communication Numbers 260709,
260710, 260711, 260712, 260713, 260714, 260715, 260716, 260717, 260718, 260730, 260734,
260735, 260736, 260737, 260739, 260742, 260752 and 260755. With respect to the Bids Reports ,
Commissioner Hansen voted no on Contract Numbers 03-53-652, 03-53-698 and 03-72-747.
Commissioner Moreno voted present on Communication Numbers 260772, 260773, 260897,
260902, 260717, 260845, 260847, 260850, 260853, 260855, 260857, 260865, 260867, 260868,
260870, 260871, 260872, 260882, 260884, 260890 and 260891. With respect to the Bids Reports,
Commissioner Moreno voted present on Contract Numbers 03-53-623, 03-72-746, 03-54-699 and
03-54-703. Commissioner Peraica voted as follows: no on Communication Numbers 260889,
260716, 260718 and 260874, and present on Communication Numbers 260897, 260902, 260803,
260911 , 260713, 260735, 260842, and Claim Number 20200716 regarding Affiliated Radiologists,
Palos Emergency Medical, Ross & Hardies, Ambulatory Anesthesiology, Rush-Presbyterian-St.
Luke's, Elk Grove Cardiology Associates, Hanger Prosthetics & Orthothotics East, Health Net Plus,
Advanced Pain Centers, Physician Anesthesia Associates, Alexian Brothers and Neurosurgical
Spine & Pain Center as found in Communication Number 260862. Commissioner Quigley voted no
on Communication Number 260889. Commissioner Suffredin voted present on Communication
Number 260892. With respect to the Highway Bills, Commissioner Suffredin voted no on Section:
02-26347-02-LS regarding HNTB Corporation and Section: 02-26347-01-EG regarding HNTB
Corporation.

Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is submitting Industrial Commission Lump Sum Petition
and Order No. OO-WC-18771 in the amount of $5,000.00 and recommends its
payment. (Finance Subcommittee July 2, 2003). Attorney: Michael D. Melber, Law
Offices of Michael D. Melber.
